import pandas as pd
import datetime
pm25 = pd.read_csv(r'C:\Users\b7073931\OneDrive - Newcastle University\Dissertation\Data Processing Storymap\PM2.5.csv')

In [93]:
#convert timestamp to date-time format and set index
pm25['timestamp'] = pd.to_datetime(pm25['timestamp'])
pm25 = pm25.sort_values(by=['timestamp'])
pm25 = pm25.set_index(pm25['timestamp'])

#set start and end date
start_date = '2020-01-04'
end_date = '2020-01-05'
mask = (pm25['timestamp'] >= start_date) & (pm25['timestamp'] < end_date)
pm25 = pm25.loc[mask]
pm25.head()

Cleaning data and removing outliers¶

In [94]:
#remove possible error measurements (outliers)
pm25 = pm25.loc[pm25['value'] > 0 ]

#remove unwanted columns
pm25.drop(["Unnamed: 0"], axis = 1, inplace = True)
pm25.drop(["timestamp"], axis = 1, inplace = True)

Checking data distribution and satistics¶

Data statistics¶

In [95]:
#checking data type at each column
pm25.info()

#find summary statistics for each sensor seperately
grp = pm25.groupby('sensor_id')

for item, itemdf in grp:
    print(item) #item is the index(sensor id)
    print(itemdf) #the data for each index
    print("skewness" , itemdf['value'].skew(axis = 0, skipna = True))
    stats = itemdf['value'].describe()
    print(stats)
    print(" ")

Comparing accuracy of AQmesh sensor with monitor¶

In [98]:
import pandas as pd
import requests
import io

#fetching and reading csv file from Github, file contains 1 week PM2.5 data starting from 1/7/2020 
url = "https://raw.githubusercontent.com/larax23/Processing-Storymap/main/PM2.5_aqmeshapi_week_raw.csv" 
df = pd.read_csv(url)
df.head(50)

#extracing a Monitor sensor
monitor = df[df['Sensor Name'].str.contains("MONITOR1135100")]

#extracting 3 close by Mesh sensors
mesh1 = df[df['Sensor Name'].str.contains("MESH1761150")]
mesh2 = df[df['Sensor Name'].str.contains("MESH1765150")]
mesh3 = df[df['Sensor Name'].str.contains("MESH1762150")]
In [99]:
monitor = monitor.loc[monitor.Variable == 'PM2.5',['Timestamp','Value']]
monitor['Timestamp'] = pd.to_datetime(monitor['Timestamp'].astype(str)) + pd.DateOffset(minutes=1) #add one minute to align it with mesh
monitor.head()

In [103]:
#merge four values into one table based on timestamp
merged = pd.merge(mesh1,mesh2, on = "Timestamp",how = "inner")
merged = pd.merge(merged,mesh3, on  = "Timestamp", how = 'inner')
merged = merged.iloc[1: , :] #remove first column from mesh datasets to align the timestamps with the monitor timestamps
merged = pd.merge(merged,monitor, on  = "Timestamp", how = 'inner')
merged.head(50)
merged = merged.set_index(merged['Timestamp'])
merged.drop(["Timestamp"], axis = 1, inplace = True)
merged.columns = ['Mesh1','Mesh2', 'Mesh3', 'Monitor']
merged.head(50)

Correlation between AQMesh and Monitor¶

In [104]:
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import numpy as np
%matplotlib inline

#Find their correlation matrix
import seaborn as sn
corr_matrix = merged.corr()

data = {'A': corr_matrix.Mesh1,
        'B': corr_matrix.Mesh2,
        'C': corr_matrix.Mesh3,
        'D': corr_matrix.Monitor
        }
df = pd.DataFrame(data,columns=['A','B','C','D'])
sn.heatmap(corr_matrix, annot=True, fmt='.3f')
